## Domain Knowledge (LLM-generated)
**Domain**: chemical reaction kinetics
**Analysis**: This task models the rate of change of concentration dA/dt as a function of concentration A and time t. Classical chemical kinetics relates reaction rates to powers of concentration (rate laws), with possible time-dependent forcing or complex mechanisms like autocatalysis or reversible reactions.

**Common formula structures in this domain**:
- Zero-order rate law: dA_dt = c0 (constant rate, independent of concentration)
- First-order rate law: dA_dt = c0 * A (radioactive decay, first-order decomposition)
- Second-order rate law: dA_dt = c0 * A**2 (bimolecular reaction of same species)
- nth-order rate law: dA_dt = c0 * A**c1 (generalized power-law kinetics)
- Reversible first-order: dA_dt = c0 * A + c1 (approach to equilibrium, A_eq = -c1/c0)
- Mixed order / two-term rate: dA_dt = c0 * A + c1 * A**2 (competing first and second order pathways)
- Autocatalytic with depletion: dA_dt = c0 * A * (c1 - A) (logistic-type autocatalysis)
- Michaelis-Menten type: dA_dt = c0 * A / (c1 + A) (enzyme-catalyzed or saturation kinetics)
- Time-dependent first-order: dA_dt = c0 * A * exp(c1 * t) (time-varying rate constant, e.g., temperature ramp)
- Oscillatory forcing: dA_dt = c0 * A + c1 * sin(c2 * t) (periodically driven reaction system)
- Power-law with time dependence: dA_dt = c0 * A**c1 * t**c2 (dispersive kinetics in heterogeneous media)
- Cooperative kinetics (Hill-type): dA_dt = c0 * A**c1 / (c2 + A**c1) (cooperative binding/reaction)
- Third-order rate law: dA_dt = c0 * A**3 (trimolecular or effective third-order kinetics)
- Linear combination with offset: dA_dt = c0 * A**2 + c1 * A + c2 (polynomial rate law from complex mechanism)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Negative proportionality to concentration (dA_dt = -k*A^n) indicates simple consumption/decay kinetics with order n
- A rate expression of form A*(c - A) suggests autocatalytic or logistic growth where the species catalyzes its own production up to a carrying capacity
- Rational forms like A/(K+A) indicate enzyme saturation or Langmuir-type surface coverage limiting the rate
- Explicit time dependence in rate laws suggests non-isothermal conditions, photochemical intensity changes, or catalyst deactivation over time
- Fractional reaction orders (A**c with non-integer c) often arise from complex multi-step mechanisms or heterogeneous catalysis
- A sum of terms with different powers of A (e.g., c0*A + c1*A**2) indicates parallel reaction pathways with different molecularities
- Sign of the leading coefficient determines consumption (negative) vs. production (positive) of species A
- If dA_dt depends on A but not t, the system is autonomous and solutions are determined solely by initial conditions
- Polynomial expressions in A that factor as A*(A-c1)*(A-c2) indicate multiple steady states and bistability in the reaction network

GT: -c0*A**c1 - c2*A*exp(-c3*_s*t) + c4*_w*cos(log(A + c5))
Candidate formulas: 50

I need to find a candidate that can match the GT:
`-0.5475*A² - 0.5475*A*exp(-0.03708*t) + 0.7049*cos(log(A + 1))`

The GT has three terms:
1. A quadratic term: `-0.5475*A²`
2. An exponential decay times A: `-0.5475*A*exp(-0.03708*t)`
3. A cosine of log term: `0.7049*cos(log(A + 1))`

Let me look for candidates that can produce a `cos(log(A + ...))` term, since that's the most distinctive part.

**Candidate 11**: `A²*c0*exp(c1*t) + A*c2 + c3*exp(c4*t) + c5 + c6*sin(c7*log(A*c8 + 1) + c9)`

Setting c1=0: `A²*c0 + A*c2 + c3*exp(c4*t) + c5 + c6*sin(c7*log(A*c8 + 1) + c9)`

Using the identity sin(x + π/2) = cos(x), I can write `c6*sin(c7*log(A*c8+1) + c9) = c6*cos(c7*log(A*c8+1))` when c9 = -π/2 and c7=1, c8=1.

But I still need `A*exp(-0.03708*t)`. Here I have `c3*exp(c4*t)` which doesn't have the A factor. So this doesn't work.

**Candidate 34**: `A*c0 + c1 + c2*exp(c3*t)*log(A*c4 + 1) + c5*sin(c6*log(A*c7 + 1) + c8)`

This has `sin(c6*log(A*c7+1) + c8)` which can become `cos(log(A+1))` with c6=1, c7=1, c8=π/2. But it lacks an A² term and has `A*c0` instead. The `c2*exp(c3*t)*log(A*c4+1)` term can't produce `A*exp(...)`. Not a match.

**Candidate 6**: `A²*c0*exp(c1*t) + A*c2 + A^c3*c4/(A^c3 + c5) + c6 + c7*exp(c8*t)*log(A*c9 + 1)`

No cos/sin term. Can't match.

**Candidate 28**: `A*c0*exp(c1*t) + A*c2 + A + c3*exp(c1*t) + c4 + c5*exp(c6*sin(A*c7 + c8))`

The sin is inside an exp, not matching cos(log(...)).

**Candidate 9**: `A*c0*exp(c1*t) + A*c2*exp(c3*t)/(A + c4) + c5 + c6*exp(c7*sin(A*c8 + c9))`

Again sin inside exp.

**Candidate 19**: `A²*c0*exp(c1*t) + A*c2*exp(c1*t) + A*c3 + A + c4*exp(c5*t) + c6`

No trig/log terms. Can't match cos(log(A+1)).

Let me reconsider candidate 11 more carefully:
`A²*c0*exp(c1*t) + A*c2 + c3*exp(c4*t) + c5 + c6*sin(c7*log(A*c8 + 1) + c9)`

The GT needs `-0.5475*A*exp(-0.03708*t)`. This candidate has no `A*exp(t)` term. It has `A*c2` (no t-dependence) and `c3*exp(c4*t)` (no A-dependence). These can't combine to give `A*exp(t)`.

None of the candidates seem to have both:
1. A term that can produce `cos(log(A+1))` or equivalent
2. A term `A*exp(αt)`

Only candidates 11 and 34 have sin/cos of log, and neither has `A*exp(αt)`.

After exhaustive search, no candidate can simultaneously produce all three terms of the GT: `A²`, `A*exp(αt)`, and `cos(log(A+1))`.

GT Equivalence Verification (CRK3)

GT: -c0*A**c1 - c2*A*exp(-c3*_s*t) + c4*_w*cos(log(A + c5))
Candidates evaluated: 50

I need to compare each candidate against the Ground Truth (GT):

**GT:** `-0.5475*A² - 0.5475*A*exp(-0.03708*t) + 0.7049*cos(log(A + 1))`

The GT has three distinct basis functions:
1. `A²` (polynomial)
2. `A*exp(αt)` (exponential decay times A)
3. `cos(log(A + 1))` (cosine of logarithm)

The key challenge is that `cos(log(A+1))` is a very specific transcendental function. Let me check which candidates could possibly reproduce this.

**Analysis of the cos(log(A+1)) term:**
This function is NOT equivalent to any polynomial, exponential, rational function, `sin(A)`, `exp(A)`, `log(A+1)`, or simple combinations thereof. It requires either:
- An explicit `cos(log(...))` term, or
- A `sin(log(...) + phase)` term (since sin(x + π/2) = cos(x))

Let me scan candidates for terms that could match `cos(log(A+1))`:

- **Candidate 11:** Has `sin(c7*log(A*c8 + 1) + c9)` — this could match `cos(log(A+1))` by setting c7=1, c8=1, c9=π/2. Also has `A²*exp(c1*t)` which can give `-0.5475*A²` if c1=0, `A*c2` for the linear A part, `c3*exp(c4*t)` and `c5`. But wait — the GT has `A*exp(αt)`, not just `A`. Let me check: GT has `-0.5475*A*exp(-0.03708*t)`. Candidate 11 has `A*c2` (no exponential in t for the A term). There's `c3*exp(c4*t)` but that's not multiplied by A. So candidate 11 cannot produce `A*exp(αt)`. **NO MATCH.**

- **Candidate 34:** Has `c5*sin(c6*log(A*c7 + 1) + c8)` — can match `cos(log(A+1))`. Also has `c2*exp(c3*t)*log(A*c4 + 1)` and `A*c0 + c1`. The GT needs `A*exp(αt)`, but this candidate has `exp(c3*t)*log(A*c4+1)` instead. These are different basis functions — `A*exp(αt)` vs `log(A+1)*exp(αt)`. These cannot be made equal for all A. **NO MATCH.**

- **Candidate 9:** Has `c6*exp(c7*sin(A*c8 + c9))` — this is `exp(sin(...))`, not `cos(log(...))`. **NO MATCH.**

- **Candidate 19:** Has `c3*sin(A*c4 + c5)` — this is `sin(linear in A)`, not `cos(log(A+1))`. **NO MATCH.**

- **Candidate 28:** Has `c5*exp(c6*sin(A*c7 + c8))` — `exp(sin(...))`, not matching. **NO MATCH.**

Going through all other candidates: Most contain only polynomials in A, exponentials in t, exponentials in A, rational functions, `log(A+1)`, or `log(A²+1)`. None of these can reproduce `cos(log(A+1))`.

Let me verify candidates 11 and 34 more carefully were the only ones with sin/cos of log terms, and confirm no others have this structure.

Scanning all 50 candidates... Only candidates 11 and 34 have `sin(...log(...))` type terms. Both fail because they can't reproduce `A*exp(αt)`.

Wait — Candidate 11: `A²c0*exp(c1*t) + A*c2 + c3*exp(c4*t) + c5 + c6*sin(c7*log(A*c8+1)+c9)`. If c1=0, we get `A²c0`. We need `A*exp(αt)` but only have `A*c2`. We can't get the time-dependent A term. **NO MATCH.**

No candidate has both `cos(log(A+1))` (or equivalent) AND `A*exp(αt)`.
